	focus = {
		id = GER_soviet_war
		icon = GFX_focus_attack_soviet
		will_lead_to_war_with = SOV
		x = 9
		y = 19
		cost = 6
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_army_manpower = { size > 1499999 }	
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				GER = {
					is_neighbor_of  = SOV
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					has_war_with = FRA
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = GER_french_escapes
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = {
					target = SOV
					value > 100
				}	
			}
			modifier = {
				GER = {
					has_country_flag = GER_french_escapes
				}
				factor = 4
			}
			modifier = {
				FRA = {
					controls_state = 16
				}
				GER = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = GER_east_is_first # Custom Rule
					}
				}
				factor = 0.25
			}
			modifier = {
				GER = {
					surrender_progress > 0.25
				}
				factor = 0.1
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				GER = {
					has_country_flag = GER_east_is_first # Custom Rule
				}
			}
		}
		
		bypass = {
			GER = {
				OR = {
					has_war_with = SOV
					SOV = { is_puppet_of = GER }
					SOV = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
					SOV = { exists = no }
				}
			}
		}
		
		available = {
			has_army_manpower = { size > 1000000 }
		}
		
		prerequisite = {
			focus = GER_baltic_front
			focus = GER_polish_claims
			focus = GER_belarus_front
			focus = GER_ukraine_front
		}

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GER_soviet_war"
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER = {
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				219 = {
					controller = {
						GER = {
							create_wargoal = {
								type = annex_everything
								target = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}	
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					GER = {
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				219 = {
					controller = {
						GER = {
							declare_war_on = {
								type = annex_everything
								target = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}	
			}
		}
	}
